## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Created: Create PartToContainer
    Created --> SettingSolutionId: Set solution_id
    SettingSolutionId --> SettingPartId: Set part_id
    SettingPartId --> SettingContainerId: Set container_id
    SettingContainerId --> Validating: Call validate()
    Validating --> ValidationError: Missing fields or id set
    Validating --> Valid: All checks pass
    ValidationError --> [*]
    Valid --> [*]
```
